<page no="27">
<heading>
A
GLOSSARY 
Of Lancashire <f type="i">Words</f> and <f type="i">Phrases</f>:
Containing, about 900 Words more than were in any former
Impressions; in which, many of the useless Corruptions are
omitted, and wherein the Reader may observe,

<f type="i">The words mark'd</f> {A.S. Bel. Br. Da. Du. Fr. Sw. Teu} <f type="i">come from the</f> {Anglo-Saxon. Belgic. British. Danish. Dutch. French. Swedish. Tuetonic.}
</heading>
